At disposal of the guest there is also a washing machine, a dry COL neighborhood_overview VAL The Poble Nou district is part of Barcelona's coastline, it's located a few minutes (or five metro stops on the yellow line) from the centre of Barcelona. Staying in Poblenou is a great option, because you can enjoy all the benefits of a quiet neighbourhood when you need a break, visit the beach, and still benefit from being close to the city centre. The main street of the neighbourhood is Rambla del Poblenou, a classic Catalan rambla that takes you from 'Parc del Clot' right down to Bogatell beach. Ideal for a pleasant stroll. There are two wonderful beaches that line the shores of Poblenou, they are Bogatell (popular amongst the older crowd) and Mar Bella (popular amongst the younger crowd). They are top quality beaches and many of the locals appreciate them more so than the famous and touristic Barceloneta.
